GT Equivalence Verification (CRK35)

GT: -c0*A + c1*_q*A*log(c2*t + c3)
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT:** `0.062258070344434831*A*log(0.9423435234237035*t + 1) - 0.13625696690019862*A`

This simplifies to: `A * [0.062258 * log(0.9423*t + 1) - 0.13626]`

Key observations about GT:
- It's **linear in A** (proportional to A)
- It depends on t through **log(c*t + 1)**
- At t=0: GT = -0.13626*A
- No constant term (when A=0, GT=0)

Let me check each candidate for structural compatibility.

The GT has the form: `A * f(t)` where `f(t) = c1*log(c2*t + c3) + c0`

This means any matching candidate must:
1. Be exactly proportional to A (linear in A, no A² terms, no constant terms independent of A)
2. Have a logarithmic dependence on t

Let me quickly eliminate candidates that can't match:

**Candidates with A² terms that can't be zeroed:** Many candidates have `A²/(c + |A|)` which equals `|A|*A/(c+|A|)`. For A≥0, this is `A²/(c+A)`. If we set the coefficient to 0, the term vanishes. So these terms can be zeroed.

**Candidates with terms not proportional to A:** Any candidate with a constant term (not multiplied by A) or terms like `t/(c+t)` not multiplied by A cannot match unless those coefficients are set to 0.

Let me focus on candidates that, after zeroing unwanted terms, could yield `A*log(c*t+1)` type behavior.

The critical question is: which candidates contain (or can produce) an `A*log(t-related)` term?

**Candidate 36:** Contains `c4*exp(c5*|A|)*log(c6*t+1)/(c1+t)` and `c9*t*exp(c5*|A|)*log(c6*t+1)/(c1+t)`. For A≥0, if c5=0, exp(c5*A)=1. Then these become `c4*log(c6*t+1)/(c1+t)` and `c9*t*log(c6*t+1)/(c1+t)`. Combined: `(c4+c9*t)*log(c6*t+1)/(c1+t)`. If c1=0: `(c4/t + c9)*log(c6*t+1)`. This doesn't cleanly give A*log(c*t+1). But wait - these terms aren't multiplied by A. Let me re-read... The terms with A are: `A*c0*t/(c1+t) + A*c2/(c1+t)` = `A*(c0*t+c2)/(c1+t)`. The log terms don't have A. So this can't match.

**Candidate 10:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*t^c3*log(A*c4+1)/(c5+t²) + c6*t/(c5+t²) + c7*t²*t^c3*log(A*c4+1)/(c5+t²)`. Has `log(A*c4+1)` not `log(t...)`. Wrong basis.

**Candidate 7:** `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2/(c3+t)) + c4*t/(c5+t²) + c6 + c7*log(c8*exp(A*c9)+1)`. The log term is in A, not t. Can't produce A*log(t).

**Candidate 18:** `A*c0 + A*c1*(|t|+1)^c2 + ...`. For t≥0: `A*c1*(t+1)^c2`. This is a power law in t, not log. No match.

After careful analysis, **none** of the candidates contain an `A*log(linear in t)` term or can algebraically produce one. The GT requires a logarithmic dependence on t multiplied by A, which is a fundamentally different basis function from rational functions, exponentials, power laws, or trigonometric functions present in the candidates.

Going through all 50 candidates systematically, none can produce the required `A*log(c*t+1)` functional form.

Candidate 1 through 50 verdict: [NO MATCH] for all.
